The naughty castle is not small, with few people, clean, and good protection measures. It is safe and secure. There are also small trains and electric cars outdoors. The swimming pool is also quite large, divided into many areas, and adults and children can play separately, which is very good. The infinity pool is very good for taking pictures. 4. The buffet dinner is 238 yuan, which is good value for money. 5. There is a special takeaway area on the first floor of the hotel, which is much better than Westin's only putting it on the ground. It is not convenient for me to take food with my child alone. The housekeeper Xiao Cai also arranged for his colleagues to deliver it to my room. I really want to give them a thumbs up! Disadvantages: 1. Maybe it is because the hotel is newly developed and the greening is too good. Two small insects and a large flying insect were found in the room. I hope the hotel can do it once a day. Westin did a better job in this regard. I didn't see a single bug in the room during my stay. 2. The switch instructions for the room lights are unclear. The bathroom lights cannot be turned on separately, and the spotlights on the bed cannot be turned off, which is not very user-friendly. 3. Outside the buffet restaurant on the first floor, there are emcees hosting activities and stage performances at night. The sound is really loud, although I can't hear it in my room. It is recommended to change the activities to the banquet hall or other areas that will not affect the guests' rest. Summary: Recommended to stay

msg:The worst experience of this Hainan trip! Please avoid pitfalls.
1. There was no concierge reception at the hotel entrance at 13:30, and the order was a bit messy. At 40, I went to the front desk to check in to room 701. The front desk said that there was a concierge to help with the luggage. I waited for two minutes because the lobby was too hot. In the end, I had to move to room 701 by myself.
2. The temperature in room 701 was 28 degrees without pre-opening the air conditioner. It was hot. Not long after turning on the air conditioner, I turned it off by myself. I received a call from the front desk saying that there was a fault alarm. Then I contacted the housekeeper and moved to room 601 because there was a problem with the air conditioner.
3. I moved my luggage to room 601 by myself. The air conditioner was not turned on in advance. The room was 28 degrees. I thought about turning on the air conditioner to cool the room. The room was stuffy and I couldn‚Äôt stay there, so I went out (the stuffiness was because if the balcony window was opened, the air conditioner would stop running, so the room was like a sauna). At 15:47, I returned to room 601 and it showed 27 degrees (as shown in the picture). I contacted the housekeeper to explain that there was a problem with the air conditioner and started repairs. I found the sweaty floor aunt to get children's slippers by myself. At 16:42, the master finished the repair and asked me to observe for an hour. The child was sweating profusely, and the family of three was steaming in the sauna. At this time, the air conditioner was set to 16 degrees, the room temperature was 27 degrees, and the outlet temperature was 21.6 degrees (as shown in the picture).
4. Contact the housekeeper to report that the air conditioner was not repaired. At 17:46, I packed my luggage and moved to room 801 applied by the housekeeper again. It has been 4 hours since I checked in and moved into the third room.
5. The air conditioner in room 801 was not pre-opened. Because the room was stuffy, I went out and returned at 19:07. The air conditioner showed that the set temperature was 16 degrees and the room temperature was 28 degrees (as shown in the picture).
6. After contacting the housekeeper, the duty manager led the team to the site for repair. Here is the key point, [the duty manager said that the room will automatically cut off the power when it detects that someone has left]. Can you bear this? Regardless of whether it is high-tech energy-saving and emission-reduction, is it reasonable for the hotel? It means that guests should steam sauna first after checking in and wait for the temperature to drop, and be prepared to steam again after going out and returning? Is there anyone who understands it?
7. It was not repaired until about 7:30. The child was hungry and wanted to go out for dinner. The hotel staff wanted to continue repairing the room and said they would give an explanation after the repair. At 20:35, I received a call from the duty manager and was told that I needed to change the room again, to a room described by the manager as [a room where the air conditioner can work normally]. At 22:22, I returned to the lobby to contact the duty manager. At 24, the room card failed and I was trapped outside the door of 801 (as shown). I waited at the door for at least 5 minutes in sweat. The service staff came to help move the luggage to room 543.
8. The air conditioner in room 543 was pre-opened and could operate normally for cooling. The luggage was put away at 22:42 (as shown). From the time I checked in to the time I moved into the fourth room, 9 hours had passed. Here is a question, why is the high-tech [automatic power off when detecting that someone has left] not applicable to room 543?
9. After the problem in the third room, I have contacted Ctrip to assist in handling it, but the information obtained by Ctrip from contacting the hotel is inconsistent with the actual result of the hotel's handling, and the hotel feedback that the reason for my room change has nothing to do with their air conditioner not working properly? ! Fortunately, I have kept the evidence, and Ctrip can handle it fairly.
10. During the whole process, the housekeeper was responsive and actively communicated, but the hotel engineering maintenance depar**ent and the duty manager‚Äôs statement that the air conditioner could not operate normally was incredible! If the intelligent engineering cannot bring users a convenient and comfortable experience, what is the meaning of its existence? This is not an excuse for facility failure.
11. The hotel is divided into the east wing and the west wing. The air conditioner in the west is a little cooler than that in the east, but the body feels hot everywhere. Compared with the aesthetics of architectural design, is it the basis for a hotel to pay attention to ensuring the appropriate temperature?
12. In rooms 801 and 543, the toilet and shower room share a pullable transparent glass door, and the partition area is also transparent. Is it inconvenient for the child to grow up? If you take a shower and squat at the same time, what kind of eyes do you use to look at each other? Who is this door suitable for?
13. The hotel breakfast is very, very ordinary. The dining area is large but there are not many varieties. There is only one kind of dessert similar to wife cake. I saw a dessert cabinet but it was not open, and the rest is bread.
14. The v park is quite big but the air conditioning is not enough. In the afternoon of check-in, the children could not participate in the reserved games because of the constant room change. The anti-slip socks are 10 yuan a pair, and the game machine needs to buy coins separately.
15. I went to the water fortress after changing rooms and waiting for the air conditioning to cool down. The water was very cold after 6 o'clock, and there were floating objects on the water surface.
16. There is a beach, but I didn't have time to go.
17. When I changed to 801, the housekeeper sent fruits, children's dolls and bumper car experience coupons. When I changed to 543, the fruit plate was in 801.
18. During the stay, I encountered families with children and luggage complaining about changing rooms many times. I don't know why.
19. 543 is a pool room. You can play when there is no sun. The housekeeper applied for a late check-out to compete with the sun.
Finally, if you are going to stay in this hotel for a trip, I hope you don't have the same luck as me, changing rooms and steaming saunas for most of the day.

The room service is remarkable, the waiter Dong Jinlong is thoughtful and efficient, and the personalized suggestions are very considerate, which directly improves the comfort of staying and makes up for the shortcomings of the size of the big bed. If you are lucky, you can also experience the original ecological environment of the hotel. Occasionally, some small insects or spiders will come to visit. After all, it is relatively close to the coconut forest, and the small insects can visit by flying, which is another adventure. The beach is very close to the hotel. The sand is soft, the color is milky white, the waves are relatively large, and the sound of the waves is still there. It is worthy of the title of singing beach. V Paradise is one of the highlights of the hotel. During the most exciting hours of the sun, it provides a space for children to let go. If the bracelet is integrated into the room card, it will be more perfect to put a label on the place. After all, the hand The ring is easy to lose, which is not very convenient. The breakfast room may be a disadvantage of staying in. The restaurant has a large area and there are many service staff, but I feel that there is still room for improvement in service efficiency. I have seen several waiters clean up a table together many times, while other tables are still waiting to be cleaned. There are many. There seem to be a lot of food options, but the categories are not rich, and the food placement is scattered. But as far as drinks are concerned, there is one place for cold drinks, another place for hot and cold milk, another place for coffee, and another place for porridge and liquid food. In more places, the food in the pastry area is scattered everywhere, hoping to make a more effective layout and improve the perception of diners. In addition, the hotel's network feels average during this stay. The room network is intermittent, but the overall speed is okay. There are blind spots in the corridor and public area network coverage, which can be further improved. The east side of the hotel is still under construction, because the distance is far away, the overall impact can be ignored. In general, the check-in experience is good, the service ability is very good, it is worth recommending.
